        <h3 class="block__title">
         Our Products
        </h3>
        <div class="block__content">
         <div class="sb_front_row homepage-our-prod-container">
          <a class="sb_front_col col_one" href="/about/publishing-partnerships">
           <div class="sb_front_icon">
            <p class="our-prod-sub-img">
             <img alt="" src="sites/all/themes/smartbrief_3/images/Image2020SBWEB-2011_Products_Newsletter.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="sb_front_content-wrp">
            <div class="sb_front_header">
             <h2 class="our-prod-header">
              Custom Newsletters
             </h2>
            </div>
            <div class="sb_front_desc">
             <p class="our-prod-content">
              Created with a combination of technology, editorial expertise and industry knowledge, SmartBrief's custom newsletters curate timely and relevant news to keep busy professionals on top of the trends and best practices that are shaping their fields.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
           <p>
           </p>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a class="sb_front_col col_two" href="/smartstudio">
           <div class="sb_front_icon">
            <p class="our-prod-sub-img">
             <img alt="" src="sites/all/themes/smartbrief_3/images/Image2020SBWEB-2011_Products_SmartStudio.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="sb_front_content-wrp">
            <div class="sb_front_header">
             <h2 class="our-prod-header">
              SmartStudio
             </h2>
            </div>
            <div class="sb_front_desc">
             <p class="our-prod-content">
              SmartStudio combines SmartBrief's expertise and engaged network of readers interests with your brand messaging. Our team of editorial experts, creative designers and project managers will guide you through the content creation process from ideation to distribution.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
           <p>
           </p>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a class="sb_front_col col_three" href="/about/advertising">
           <div class="sb_front_icon">
            <p class="our-prod-sub-img">
             <img alt="" src="sites/all/themes/smartbrief_3/images/Image2020SBWEB-2011_Products_TargetedAd.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="sb_front_content-wrp">
            <div class="sb_front_header">
             <h2 class="our-prod-header">
              Targeted Advertising
             </h2>
            </div>
            <div class="sb_front_desc">
             <p class="our-prod-content">
              Visibility, expertise and relevance - the hallmarks of an industry leader. By distributing the right mix of advertising and content you will get the best of all three, with your name and insights delivered alongside the industry's most important news.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
           <p>
           </p>
          </a>
